269→func handleRootHealth(name string, firstTimeHealthy func(), checks ...HealthChecker) http.HandlerFunc {\n   270→\tvar notifyOnce sync.Once\n   271→\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   272→\t\texcluded := getExcludedChecks(r)\n   273→\t\tunknownExcluded := excluded.Clone()\n   274→\t\t// failedVerboseLogOutput is for output to the log.  It indicates detailed failed output information for the log.\n   275→\t\tvar failedVerboseLogOutput bytes.Buffer\n   276→\t\tvar failedChecks []string\n   277→\t\tvar individualCheckOutput bytes.Buffer\n   278→\t\tfor _, check := range checks {\n   279→\t\t\t// no-op the check if we've specified we want to exclude the check\n   280→\t\t\tif excluded.Has(check.Name()) {\n   281→\t\t\t\tunknownExcluded.Delete(check.Name())\n   282→\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&individualCheckOutput, \"[+]%s excluded: ok\\n\", check.Name())\n   283→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   284→\t\t\t}\n   285→\t\t\t// no-op the check if it is a grouped check and we want to exclude the group\n   286→\t\t\tif check, ok := check.(GroupedHealthChecker); ok && excluded.Has(check.GroupName()) {\n   287→\t\t\t\tunknownExcluded.Delete(check.GroupName())\n   288→\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&individualCheckOutput, \"[+]%s excluded with %s: ok\\n\", check.Name(), check.GroupName())\n   289→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   290→\t\t\t}\n   291→\t\t\tif err := check.Check(r); err != nil {\n   292→\t\t\t\tslis.ObserveHealthcheck(context.Background(), check.Name(), name, slis.Error)\n   293→\t\t\t\t// don't include the error since this endpoint is public. charset=utf-8\")\n   323→\t\tw.Header().Set(\"X-Content-Type-Options\", \"nosniff\")\n   324→\t\tif _, found := r.URL.Query()[\"verbose\"]; !found {\n   325→\t\t\tfmt.Fprint(w, \"ok\")\n   326→\t\t\treturn\n   327→\t\t}\n   328→\n   329→\t\tindividualCheckOutput.WriteTo(w)\n   330→\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"%s check passed\\n\", name)\n   331→\t}\n   332→}\n   333→\n   334→// adaptCheckToHandler returns an http.HandlerFunc that serves the provided checks.\n   335→func adaptCheckToHandler(c func(r *http.Request) error) http.HandlerFunc {\n   336→\treturn http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   337→\t\terr := c(r)\n   338→\t\tif err != nil {\n   339→\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"internal server error: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n   340→\t\t} else {\n   341→\t\t\tfmt.Fprint(w, \"ok\")\n   342→\t\t}\n   343→\t})\n   344→}\n   345→\n   346→// checkerNames returns the names of the checks in the same order as passed in.\n   347→func checkerNames(checks ...HealthChecker) []string {\n   348→\t// accumulate the names of checks for printing them out.\n   349→\tcheckerNames := make([]string, 0, len(checks))\n   350→\tfor _, check := range checks {\n   351→\t\tcheckerNames = append(checkerNames, check.Name())\n   352→\t}\n   353→\treturn checkerNames\n   354→}\n   355→\n   356→// formatQuoted returns a formatted string of the health check names,\n   357→// preserving the order passed in.\n   358→func formatQuoted(names ...string) string {\n   359→\tquoted := make([]string, 0, len(names))\n   360→\tfor _, name := range names {\n   361→\t\tquoted = append(quoted, fmt.Sprintf(\"%q\", name))\n   362→\t}\n   363→\treturn strings.Join(quoted, \",\")\n   364→}\n   365→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. It indicates detailed failed output information for the log.\n\t\tvar failedVerboseLogOutput bytes.Buffer\n\t\tvar failedChecks []string\n\t\tvar individualCheckOutput bytes.Buffer\n\t\tfor _, check := range checks {\n\t\t\t// no-op the check if we've specified we want to exclude the check\n\t\t\tif excluded.Has(check.Name()) {\n\t\t\t\tunknownExcluded.Delete(check.Name())\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&individualCheckOutput, \"[+]%s excluded: ok\\n\", check.Name())\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// no-op the check if it is a grouped check and we want to exclude the group\n\t\t\tif check, ok := check.(GroupedHealthChecker); ok && excluded.Has(check.GroupName()) {\n\t\t\t\tunknownExcluded.Delete(check.GroupName())\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&individualCheckOutput, \"[+]%s excluded with %s: ok\\n\", check.Name(), check.GroupName())\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif err := check.Check(r); err != nil {\n\t\t\t\tslis.ObserveHealthcheck(context.Background(), check.Name(), name, slis.Error)\n\t\t\t\t// don't include the error since this endpoint is public.  If someone wants more detail\n\t\t\t\t// they should have explicit permission to the detailed checks.\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&individualCheckOutput, \"[-]%s failed: reason withheld\\n\", check.Name())\n\t\t\t\t// but we do want detailed information for our log\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&failedVerboseLogOutput, \"[-]%s failed: %v\\n\", check.Name(), err)\n\t\t\t\tfailedChecks = append(failedChecks, check.Name())\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\tslis.ObserveHealthcheck(context.Background(), check.Name(), name, slis.Success)\n\t\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&individualCheckOutput, \"[+]%s ok\\n\", check.Name())\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tif unknownExcluded.Len() > 0 {\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(&individualCheckOutput, \"warn: some health checks cannot be excluded: no matches for %s\\n\", formatQuoted(unknownExcluded.List()...))\n\t\t\tklog.V(6).Infof(\"cannot exclude some health checks, no health checks are installed matching %s\",\n\t\t\t\tformatQuoted(unknownExcluded.List()...))\n\t\t}\n\t\t// always be verbose on failure\n\t\tif len(failedChecks) > 0 {\n\t\t\tklog.V(2).Infof(\"%s check failed: %s\\n%v\", strings.Join(failedChecks, \",\"), name, failedVerboseLogOutput.String())\n\t\t\thttplog.SetStacktracePredicate(r.Context(), func(int) bool { return false })\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s%s check failed\", individualCheckOutput.String(), name), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// signal first time this is healthy\n\t\tif firstTimeHealthy != nil {\n\t\t\tnotifyOnce.Do(firstTimeHealthy)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/plain; charset=utf-8\")\n\t\tw.Header().Set(\"X-Content-Type-Options\", \"nosniff\")\n\t\tif _, found := r.URL.Query()[\"verbose\"]; !found {\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprint(w, \"ok\")\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tindividualCheckOutput.WriteTo(w)\n\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"%s check passed\\n\", name)\n\t}\n}\n\n// adaptCheckToHandler returns an http.HandlerFunc that serves the provided checks.\nfunc adaptCheckToHandler(c func(r *http.Request) error) http.HandlerFunc {\n\treturn http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t\terr := c(r)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\thttp.Error(w, fmt.Sprintf(\"internal server error: %v\", err), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprint(w, \"ok\")\n\t\t}\n\t})\n}\n\n// checkerNames returns the names of the checks in the same order as passed in.\nfunc checkerNames(checks ...HealthChecker) []string {\n\t// accumulate the names of checks for printing them out.\n\tcheckerNames := make([]string, 0, len(checks))\n\tfor _, check := range checks {\n\t\tcheckerNames = append(checkerNames, check.Name())\n\t}\n\treturn checkerNames\n}\n\n// formatQuoted returns a formatted string of the health check names,\n// preserving the order passed in.\nfunc formatQuoted(names ...string) string {\n\tquoted := make([]string, 0, len(names))\n\tfor _, name := range names {\n\t\tquoted = append(quoted, fmt.Sprintf(\"%q\", name))\n\t}\n\treturn strings.Join(quoted, \",\")\n}\n","numLines":365,"startLine":1,"totalLines":365}}}

The main implementation functions are:\\n\\n- **InstallHandler()**: Registers handlers for `/healthz` endpoint (line 171)\\n- **InstallReadyzHandler()**: Registers handlers for `/readyz` endpoint (line 179)\\n- **InstallLivezHandler()**: Registers handlers for `/livez` endpoint (line 187)\\n- **InstallPathHandlerWithHealthyFunc()**: Core function that registers health checkers with optional callback (line 202)\\n\\nKubernetes implements multiple built-in health checkers:\\n\\n1. **PingHealthz**: Simple check that always returns OK (lines 52-64)\\n2. **LogHealthz**: Verifies logging is not blocked by checking if klog.Flush() completes within 2 minutes (lines 67-92)\\n3. **InformerSyncHealthz**: Checks if all informers in the cache are synced (lines 98-152)\\n4. **ShutdownHealthz**: Fails when the process receives shutdown signal (lines 115-136)\\n5. **Custom HealthCheckers**: Components add domain-specific checks (e.g., informer sync in controller-manager)\\n\\n**Component-Specific Implementations:**\\n\\n- **kube-scheduler** (`cmd/kube-scheduler/app/server.go`, lines 374-376): Registers readiness checks including `NewShutdownHealthz()`, `sched-handler-sync` (custom check), and informer sync. The `newEndpointsHandler()` function calls `InstallHandler()`, `InstallLivezHandler()`, and `InstallReadyzHandler()`.\\n\\n- **kube-proxy** (`cmd/kube-proxy/app/server.go`, line 465): Calls `healthz.InstallHandler()` with no arguments, defaulting to PingHealthz\\n\\n- **kubelet** (`pkg/kubelet/server/server.go`, lines 427-433): Installs handlers with three checks: `PingHealthz`, `LogHealthz`, and a custom `syncloop` check via `host.SyncLoopHealthCheck`\\n\\n- **kube-proxy health check** (`pkg/proxy/healthcheck/proxy_health.go`): Custom implementation with `ProxyHealthServer` that returns JSON status. Implements separate `healthzHandler` (line 219) and `livezHandler` (line 251) that check proxier synchronization status and node eligibility. Returns HTTP 503 if unhealthy, 200 if healthy.\\n\\n### Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\n**Endpoints:** `/healthz`, `/livez`, `/readyz`\\n\\nGrafana implements health endpoints in two main locations:\\n\\n1. **pkg/server/health.go**: Defines the health check framework with:\\n   - **HealthNotifier** struct (lines 12-34): Thread-safe mechanism using atomic.Bool to signal readiness\\n   - **LivezHandler()** (lines 36-43): Always returns 200 OK to indicate process is alive\\n   - **ReadyzHandler()** (lines 45-57): Returns 200 OK if `HealthNotifier.IsReady()` is true, otherwise 503 Service Unavailable\\n   - **RegisterHealthEndpoints()** (lines 61-64): Registers both endpoints on router with GET methods\\n\\n2. **pkg/api/http_server.go**: Implements basic `/healthz` health check\\n   - **healthzHandler** (around line 756): Middleware handler that returns 200 OK if request method is GET/HEAD and path is `/healthz`\\n\\nGrafana uses a simpler model than Kubernetes, with initialization status tracked by a `HealthNotifier` that components call `SetReady()` on when they complete initialization. The `/livez` endpoint always responds with 200 OK, while `/readyz` depends on the initialization status.\\n\\n### Prometheus (prometheus/prometheus)\\n\\n**Endpoints:** `/-/healthy`, `/-/ready` (note: different naming convention with `/-/` prefix instead of `/`)\\n\\nPrometheus implements health checks in `web/web.go` with:\\n\\n1. **/-/healthy endpoint** (lines 591-597): Simple liveness check\\n   - GET handler returns 200 with message \\\"%s is Healthy.\\\"\\n   - HEAD handler returns 200 OK\\n   - Always returns healthy status (simple ping check)\\n\\n2. **/-/ready endpoint** (lines 598-604): Readiness check with state management\\n   - Wraps handler with `readyf()` function (alias for `h.testReady`)\\n   - GET handler returns 200 with message \\\"%s is Ready.\\\" only when ready\\n   - HEAD handler returns 200 OK only when ready\\n\\n**Key Implementation Details** (lines 641-677):\\n\\n- **SetReady()** (lines 642-651): Sets ready status using atomic operation (Handler.ready)\\n  - When status is `Ready`: stores uint32(Ready) and sets metrics.readyStatus to 1\\n  - Otherwise: stores status value and sets metrics.readyStatus to 0\\n\\n- **isReady()** (lines 654-656): Atomic read of ready status\\n\\n- **testReady()** (lines 659-677): Wrapper function that:\\n  - Calls handler function f if status is `Ready`\\n  - Returns 503 Service Unavailable if status is `NotReady` or `Stopping`\\n  - Sets `X-Prometheus-Stopping` header to true if stopping, false if not ready\\n\\nPrometheus manages three ready states: `Ready`, `NotReady`, and `Stopping`, allowing graceful shutdown detection. The `/-/ready` endpoint supports both GET and HEAD methods and checks the state before executing the handler.\\n\\n## Key Differences Summary\\n\\n| Feature | Kubernetes | Grafana | Prometheus |\\n|---------|------------|---------|------------|\\n| Endpoint Paths | /healthz, /livez, /readyz | /healthz, /livez, /readyz | /-/healthy, /-/ready |\\n| Main Check File | staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/healthz/ | pkg/server/health.go | web/web.go |\\n| Check Types | Plugin-based (HealthChecker interface) | Simple initialization flag | State-based (Ready/NotReady/Stopping) |\\n| DB Checks | Custom implementations per component | Not explicitly shown | Not explicitly shown |\\n| Dependencies | Informer sync, leader election, component handlers | Application initialization status | Configuration readiness |\\n| Detail Level | Supports verbose mode with per-check status | Simple OK/not-ready response | JSON state with metrics |\\n\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
